Ctrip members upgraded to a balcony room, where you can see the artificial lake from the balcony. The room is also large and has a bathtub.
The service is very good: earplugs, bathtub covers, and mosquito coils are all provided.
Transportation: It is very close to Daqishan and Tonglu Station by taxi.
Disadvantages: I had breakfast on weekdays, and there were few varieties. I saw other platforms selling breakfast coupons for 28 yuan, and the content should be imaginable.

msg:Overall it's pretty good, the room is big enough and decent, and the corridor is a bit old-fashioned. Being adjacent to Daqi Mountain and Yintai City is a geographical advantage. When I checked in, I received a free opening fruit, persimmons. The hotel can consider using mediocre fruits. Persimmons are delicious and sweet, but they attract small flying insects, which is a big psychological challenge for your first stay. Twin beds are combined into a large bed, which is perfect for children. Breakfast has to be supplemented for children, it is 60 on the first day and 20 on the second day. Breakfast felt a bit messy on the first day, but very quiet on the second day. Mainly steamed buns, bread, porridge, noodles and wontons. There are definitely poached eggs and fried dough sticks, but the coffee is not from the coffee machine, the pot is average, and I pour the milk myself, so I make do.
